  27 /* Table for Big5 to UCS conversion. This is generated from the BIG5
  28    charmap, using the following command:
  29 
  30     egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^% " | sed 's/%IRREVERSIBLE%//' | \
  31     perl segA.pl > segA
  32 
  33    where segA.pl script is:
  34 
  35   ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  36 print "static const uint16_t big5_to_ucs[13973] =\n{";
  37 while (<>) {
  38     local($ucs, $big5, %rest) = split;
  39     $ucs =~ s/<U(....)>/0x$1/;
  40     $big5 =~ s/\/x//g;
  41     $big5 = hex($big5) - 0xa140;
  42     local($ridx) = int($big5 / 256) * 157;
  43     if ($big5 % 256 > 0x3e) {
  44       $ridx += ($big5 % 256) - 0x22;
  45     } else {
  46       $ridx += ($big5 % 256);
  47     }
  48     printf "\n " if (($n % 4) == 0);
  49     ++$n;
  50     printf " [%5d] = %s,", $ridx, $ucs;
  51 }
  52 print "\n};\n";
  53 
  54 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  55 */

3539 /* The mapping from Unicode to Big5 is not easy since we have several
3540    separate blocks.  First a block of characters with the second byte
3541    being zero. */

3597 
3598 /* Tables for UCS to Big5 conversion. These are generated from the BIG5
3599    charmap, using the following commands:
3600 
3601 ---------------------------------------------------------------------
3602 rm -f segB2
3603 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U02" | sort | \
3604     perl segB2.pl 2 0x02C7 0x02D9 >> segB2
3605 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U03" | sort | \
3606     perl segB2.pl 3 0x0391 0x03C9 >> segB2
3607 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U20[1-3]" | sort | \
3608     perl segB2.pl 4 0x2013 0x203B >> segB2
3609 
3610 ( Separate U20AC, U2103, U2105, U2109 )
3611 
3612 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U216" | sort | \
3613     perl segB2.pl 5 0x2160 0x2169 >> segB2
3614 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U219" | sort | \
3615     perl segB2.pl 6 0x2190 0x2199 >> segB2
3616 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U22[1-6]" | sort | \
3617     perl segB2.pl 7 0x2215 0x2267 >> segB2
3618 
3619 ( Separate U2295, U2299, U22A5, U22BF )
3620 
3621 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U2[56]" | sort | \
3622     perl segB2.pl 8 0x2500 0x2642 >> segB2
3623 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U30" | sort | \
3624     perl segB2.pl 9 0x3000 0x3029 >> segB2
3625 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U31" | sort | \
3626     perl segB2.pl 10 0x3105 0x3129 >> segB2
3627 
3628 ( Separate U32A3 )
3629 
3630 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U33" | sort | \
3631     perl segB2.pl 11 0x338E 0x33D5 >> segB2
3632 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<U[4-9]" | sort | \
3633     perl segB2.pl 12 0x4E00 0x9FA4 >> segB2
3634 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<UF[678]" | sort | \
3635     perl segB2.pl 13 0xF6B1 0xF848 >> segB2
3636 
3637 ( Separate UFA0C, UFA0D )
3638 
3639 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<UFE" | sort | \
3640     perl segB2.pl 14 0xFE30 0xFE6B >> segB2
3641 egrep "/x../x.." BIG5 | egrep -v "^%" | egrep "^<UFF" | sort | \
3642     perl segB2.pl 15 0xFF01 0xFFE5 >> segB2
3643 ---------------------------------------------------------------------
3644 
3645    where the segB2.pl script is:
3646 
3647 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
3648 $tnum   = $ARGV[0];
3649 $ubegin = $ARGV[1];
3650 $uend   = $ARGV[2];
3651 
3652 printf("|* Table of range U+%04X - U+%04X. *|\n", hex($ubegin), hex($uend));
3653 printf("static const char from_ucs4_tab%d[][2] =\n{", $tnum);
3654 
3655 $n=0;
3656 while (<STDIN>) {
3657      local($ucs4, $big5, %rest) = split;
3658      $ucs4 =~ s/<U(....)>/$1/;
3659      $big5 =~ s/\/x//g;
3660      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
3661      local($b)=hex($big5);
3662      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 3 == 0);
3663      ++$n;
3664      printf (" [0x%04x] = \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",", $u - hex($ubegin),
3665              $b < 0x100 ? $b : int($b/256), $b < 0x100 ? 0 : $b&255);
3666 }
3667 printf ("\n};\n\n");
3668 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
3669 */
3670 
3671 /* Table of range U+02C7 - U+02D9. */
3672 static const char from_ucs4_tab2[][2] =
3673 {
3674   [0x0000] = "\xa3\xbe", [0x0002] = "\xa3\xbc", [0x0003] = "\xa3\xbd",
3675   [0x0004] = "\xa3\xbf", [0x0006] = "\xa1\xc5", [0x0012] = "\xa3\xbb",
3676 };

8353   [0x0029] = "\xa2\xd8", [0x002a] = "\xa2\xd9", [0x002b] = "\xa2\xda",
8354   [0x002c] = "\xa2\xdb", [0x002d] = "\xa2\xdc", [0x002e] = "\xa2\xdd",
8355   [0x002f] = "\xa2\xde", [0x0030] = "\xa2\xdf", [0x0031] = "\xa2\xe0",
8356   [0x0032] = "\xa2\xe1", [0x0033] = "\xa2\xe2", [0x0034] = "\xa2\xe3",
8357   [0x0035] = "\xa2\xe4", [0x0036] = "\xa2\xe5", [0x0037] = "\xa2\xe6",
8358   [0x0038] = "\xa2\xe7", [0x0039] = "\xa2\xe8", [0x003b] = "\xa2\x40",
8359   [0x003e] = "\xa1\xc4", [0x0040] = "\xa2\xe9", [0x0041] = "\xa2\xea",
8360   [0x0042] = "\xa2\xeb", [0x0043] = "\xa2\xec", [0x0044] = "\xa2\xed",
8361   [0x0045] = "\xa2\xee", [0x0046] = "\xa2\xef", [0x0047] = "\xa2\xf0",
8362   [0x0048] = "\xa2\xf1", [0x0049] = "\xa2\xf2", [0x004a] = "\xa2\xf3",
8363   [0x004b] = "\xa2\xf4", [0x004c] = "\xa2\xf5", [0x004d] = "\xa2\xf6",
8364   [0x004e] = "\xa2\xf7", [0x004f] = "\xa2\xf8", [0x0050] = "\xa2\xf9",
8365   [0x0051] = "\xa2\xfa", [0x0052] = "\xa2\xfb", [0x0053] = "\xa2\xfc",
8366   [0x0054] = "\xa2\xfd", [0x0055] = "\xa2\xfe", [0x0056] = "\xa3\x40",
8367   [0x0057] = "\xa3\x41", [0x0058] = "\xa3\x42", [0x0059] = "\xa3\x43",
8368   [0x005a] = "\xa1\x61", [0x005b] = "\xa1\x55", [0x005c] = "\xa1\x62",
8369   [0x005d] = "\xa1\xe3", [0x00df] = "\xa2\x46", [0x00e0] = "\xa2\x47",
8370   [0x00e2] = "\xa1\xc3", [0x00e4] = "\xa2\x44",
8371 };

8376 /* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function.  */
8377 #define CHARSET_NAME        "BIG5//"
8378 #define FROM_LOOP       from_big5
8379 #define TO_LOOP         to_big5
8380 #define DEFINE_INIT     1
8381 #define DEFINE_FINI     1
8382 #define MIN_NEEDED_FROM     1
8383 #define MAX_NEEDED_FROM     2
8384 #define MIN_NEEDED_TO       4
8385 #define ONE_DIRECTION       0

8387 
8388 /* First define the conversion function from Big5 to UCS4.  */
8389 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_FROM
8390 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_FROM
8391 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_TO
8392 #define LOOPFCT         FROM_LOOP
8393 #define BODY \
8394   {                                       \
8395     uint32_t ch = *inptr;                             \
8396                                           \
8397     if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xf9)                         \
8398       {                                       \
8399     /* Two-byte character.  First test whether the next byte          \
8400        is also available.  */                         \
8401     uint32_t ch2;                                 \
8402     int idx;                                  \
8403                                           \
8404     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
8405       {                                   \
8406         /* The second character is not available.  */             \
8407         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
8408         break;                                \
8409       }                                   \
8410                                           \
8411     idx = (ch - 0xa1) * 157;                          \
8412     ch2 = inptr[1];                               \
8413     /* See whether the second byte is in the correct range.  */       \
8414     if (ch2 >= 0x40 && ch2 <= 0x7e)                       \
8415       idx += ch2 - 0x40;                              \
8416     else if (__builtin_expect (ch2 >= 0xa1, 1)                \
8417          && __builtin_expect (ch2 <= 0xfe, 1))                \
8418       idx += 0x3f + (ch2 - 0xa1);                         \
8419     else                                      \
8420       {                                   \
8421         /* This is illegal.  */                       \
8422         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
8423       }                                   \
8424                                           \
8425     /* Get the value from the table.  */                      \
8426     ch = big5_to_ucs[idx];                            \
8427                                           \
8428     /* Is this character defined?  */                     \
8429     if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == 0))                       \
8430       {                                   \
8431         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
8432         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2);                   \
8433       }                                   \
8434                                           \
8435     inptr += 2;                               \
8436       }                                       \
8437     else if (ch <= 0x80)                              \
8438       ++inptr;                                    \
8439     else                                      \
8440       {                                       \
8441     /* This is illegal.  */                           \
8442     STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
8443       }                                       \
8444                                           \
8445     put32 (outptr, ch);                               \
8446     outptr += 4;                                  \
8447   }
8448 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
8449 #define ONEBYTE_BODY \
8450   {                                       \
8451     if (c <= 0x80)                                \
8452       return c;                                   \
8453     else                                      \
8454       return WEOF;                                \
8455   }
8456 #include <iconv/loop.c>
8457 
8458 
8459 /* Next, define the other direction.  */
8460 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_TO
8461 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_FROM
8462 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_FROM
8463 #define LOOPFCT         TO_LOOP
8464 #define BODY \
8465   {                                       \
8466     uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr);                          \
8467     const char *cp;                               \
8468                                           \
8469     if (__builtin_expect (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_tab1)              \
8470                  / sizeof (from_ucs4_tab1[0])), 0))       \
8471       switch (ch)                                 \
8472     {                                     \
8473         case 0x2c7 ... 0x2d9:                             \
8474       cp = from_ucs4_tab2[ch - 0x2c7];                    \
8475       break;                                  \
8476     case 0x391 ... 0x3c9:                             \
8477       cp = from_ucs4_tab3[ch - 0x391];                    \
8478       break;                                  \
8479     case 0x2013 ... 0x203b:                           \
8480       cp = from_ucs4_tab4[ch - 0x2013];                   \
8481       break;                                  \
8482     case 0x20ac:                                  \
8483       cp = "\xa3\xe1";                            \
8484       break;                                  \
8485     case 0x2103:                                  \
8486       cp = "\xa2\x4a";                            \
8487       break;                                  \
8488     case 0x2105:                                  \
8489       cp = "\xa1\xc1";                            \
8490       break;                                  \
8491     case 0x2109:                                  \
8492       cp = "\xa2\x4b";                            \
8493       break;                                  \
8494     case 0x2160 ... 0x2169:                           \
8495       cp = from_ucs4_tab5[ch - 0x2160];                   \
8496       break;                                  \
8497     case 0x2190 ... 0x2199:                           \
8498       cp = from_ucs4_tab6[ch - 0x2190];                   \
8499       break;                                  \
8500     case 0x2215 ... 0x2267:                           \
8501       cp = from_ucs4_tab7[ch - 0x2215];                   \
8502       break;                                  \
8503     case 0x2295:                                  \
8504       cp = "\xa1\xf2";                            \
8505       break;                                  \
8506     case 0x2299:                                  \
8507       cp = "\xa1\xf3";                            \
8508       break;                                  \
8509     case 0x22a5:                                  \
8510       cp = "\xa1\xe6";                            \
8511       break;                                  \
8512     case 0x22bf:                                  \
8513       cp = "\xa1\xe9";                            \
8514       break;                                  \
8515     case 0x2500 ... 0x2642:                           \
8516       cp = from_ucs4_tab8[ch - 0x2500];                   \
8517       break;                                  \
8518     case 0x3000 ... 0x3029:                           \
8519       cp = from_ucs4_tab9[ch - 0x3000];                   \
8520       break;                                  \
8521     case 0x3105 ... 0x3129:                           \
8522       cp = from_ucs4_tab10[ch - 0x3105];                      \
8523       break;                                  \
8524     case 0x32a3:                                  \
8525       cp = "\xa1\xc0";                            \
8526       break;                                  \
8527     case 0x338e ... 0x33d5:                           \
8528       cp = from_ucs4_tab11[ch - 0x338e];                      \
8529       break;                                  \
8530     case 0x4e00 ... 0x9fa4:                           \
8531       cp = from_ucs4_tab12[ch - 0x4e00];                      \
8532       break;                                  \
8533     case 0xf6b1 ... 0xf848:                           \
8534       cp = from_ucs4_tab13[ch - 0xf6b1];                      \
8535       break;                                  \
8536     case 0xfa0c:                                  \
8537       cp = "\xc9\x4a";                            \
8538       break;                                  \
8539     case 0xfa0d:                                  \
8540       cp = "\xdd\xfc";                            \
8541       break;                                  \
8542     case 0xfe30 ... 0xfe6b:                           \
8543       cp = from_ucs4_tab14[ch - 0xfe30];                      \
8544       break;                                  \
8545     case 0xff01 ... 0xffe5:                           \
8546       cp = from_ucs4_tab15[ch - 0xff01];                      \
8547       break;                                  \
8548     default:                                  \
8549       UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4);                        \
8550       /* Illegal character.  */                       \
8551       cp = "";                                \
8552       break;                                  \
8553     }                                     \
8554     else                                      \
8555       cp = from_ucs4_tab1[ch];                            \
8556                                           \
8557     if (__builtin_expect (cp[0], '\1') == '\0' && ch != 0)            \
8558       {                                       \
8559     /* Illegal character.  */                         \
8560     STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4);                     \
8561       }                                       \
8562     else                                      \
8563       {                                       \
8564     /* See whether there is enough room for the second byte we write.  */ \
8565     if (__builtin_expect (cp[1], '\1') != '\0'                \
8566         && __builtin_expect (outptr + 1 >= outend, 0))            \
8567       {                                   \
8568         /* We have not enough room.  */                   \
8569         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
8570         break;                                \
8571       }                                   \
8572                                           \
8573     *outptr++ = cp[0];                            \
8574     if (cp[1] != '\0')                            \
8575       *outptr++ = cp[1];                              \
8576       }                                       \
8577                                           \
8578     inptr += 4;                                   \
8579   }
8580 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
8581 #include <iconv/loop.c>
